.keel/epics/VFDv1i61H/voyages/VFDv3gE5m/RECURSIVE_PLANNER_PROOF.md --- Text
 1 # Recursive Planner Proof
 2 
 3 ## Implemented Backbone
 4 
 5 - Interpretation-time operator memory now includes `AGENTS.md` plus linked foundational guidance excerpts in [agent_memory.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/agent_memory.rs).
 6 - The recursive planner contract lives in [planning.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/domain/ports/planning.rs) and is rendered through typed turn events in [turns.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/domain/model/turns.rs).
 7 - The application now routes non-trivial turns through a planner-owned loop in [mod.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/application/mod.rs), with bounded `search`, `read`, `inspect`, `refine`, `branch`, and `stop` actions.
 8 - Planner and synthesizer roles are independently configurable through [main.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/main.rs) and [mod.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/application/mod.rs), with the planner adapter wired in [sift_planner.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/sift_planner.rs) and planner action selection implemented in [sift_agent.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/adapters/sift_agent.rs).
 9 - The default transcript UI now renders interpretation context, planner capability, planner actions, and planner summaries in [interactive_tui.rs](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/src/infrastructure/cli/interactive_tui.rs).
10 
11 ## Documentation Sync
12 
13 - The recursive harness backbone, current runtime lanes, and planner/synth split were updated in [README.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/README.md).
14 - The detailed implementation snapshot was updated in [ARCHITECTURE.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/ARCHITECTURE.md).
15 - Operational invariants and operator guidance were updated in [POLICY.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/POLICY.md), [AGENTS.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/AGENTS.md), [INSTRUCTIONS.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/INSTRUCTIONS.md), and [CONFIGURATION.md](/home/alex/workspace/spoke-sh/paddles/CONFIGURATION.md).
16 
17 ## Verification

20 - `cargo fmt --all --check`
21 - `just quality`

2546 ... 263 fn discover_linked_documents(agent_path: &Path, contents: &str) -> Vec<PathBuf> {
2547 ... 264     let mut ordered = Vec::new();
2548 ... 265     let mut seen = HashSet::new();
2549 ... 266     for target in extract_markdown_link_targets(contents)
2550 ... 267         .into_iter()
2551 ... 268         .chain(extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents))
2552 ... 269     {
2553 ... 270         let Some(resolved) = resolve_link_target(agent_path, &target) else {
2554 ... 271             continue;
2555 ... 272         };
2556 ... 273         let canonical = canonical_memory_path(&resolved);
2557 ... 274         if seen.insert(canonical) {
2558 ... 275             ordered.push(resolved);
2559 ... 276         }
2560 ... 277     }
2561 ... 278     ordered
2562 ... 279 }
2563 ... 280 
2564 ... 281 fn extract_markdown_link_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2565 ... 282     let mut targets = Vec::new();
2566 ... 283     let mut remainder = contents;
2567 ... 284     while let Some(start) = remainder.find("](") {
2568 ... 285         let candidate = &remainder[start + 2..];
2569 ... 286         let Some(end) = candidate.find(')') else {
2570 ... 287             break;
2571 ... 288         };
2572 ... 289         let target = candidate[..end].trim();
2573 ... 290         if !target.is_empty() {
2574 ... 291             targets.push(target.to_string());
2575 ... 292         }
2576 ... 293         remainder = &candidate[end + 1..];
2577 ... 294     }
2578 ... 295     targets
2579 ... 296 }
2580 ... 297 
2581 ... 298 fn extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2582 ... 299     let mut targets = Vec::new();
2583 ... 300     let mut in_tick = false;
2584 ... 301     let mut current = String::new();
2585 ... 302 
2586 ... 303     for ch in contents.chars() {
2587 ... 304         if ch == '`' {
2588 ... 305             if in_tick {
2589 ... 306                 let trimmed = current.trim();
2590 ... 307                 if looks_like_local_doc_target(trimmed) {
2591 ... 308                     targets.push(trimmed.to_string());
2592 ... 309                 }
2593 ... 310                 current.clear();
2594 ... 311             }
2595 ... 312             in_tick = !in_tick;
2596 ... 313             continue;
2597 ... 314         }
2598 ... 315 
2599 ... 316         if in_tick {
2600 ... 317             current.push(ch);
2601 ... 318         }
2602 ... 319     }
2603 ... 320 
2604 ... 321     targets
2605 ... 322 }
2606 ... 323 
2607 ... 324 fn looks_like_local_doc_target(target: &str) -> bool {
2608 ... 325     target.ends_with(".md") || target.starts_with(".keel/")
2609 ... 326 }
2610 ... 327 
2611 ... 328 fn resolve_link_target(agent_path: &Path, target: &str) -> Option<PathBuf> {
2612 ... 329     if target.starts_with("http://")
2613 ... 330         || target.starts_with("https://")
2614 ... 331         || target.starts_with("mailto:")
2615 ... 332     {
2616 ... 333         return None;
2617 ... 334     }
2618 ... 335 
2619 ... 336     let target = target.split('#').next()?.trim();
2620 ... 337     if target.is_empty() || !looks_like_local_doc_target(target) {
2621 ... 338         return None;
2622 ... 339     }
2623 ... 340 
2624 ... 341     let candidate = if Path::new(target).is_absolute() {
2625 ... 342         PathBuf::from(target)
2626 ... 343     } else {
2627 ... 344         agent_path.parent()?.join(target)
2628 ... 345     };
2629 ... 346 
2630 ... 347     if candidate.is_file() {
2631 ... 348         Some(candidate)
2632 ... 349     } else {
2633 ... 350         None
2634 ... 351     }
2635 ... 352 }

2637 160 354 fn trim_memory_contents(contents: &str) -> String {
2638 161 355     if contents.chars().count() <= MAX_MEMORY_FILE_CHARS {
2639

2641 170 364     trimmed

2651 ... 374 fn select_relevant_excerpt(contents: &str, user_prompt: &str) -> (String, usize) {
2652 ... 375     let query_terms = prompt_terms(user_prompt);
2653 ... 376     let lines = contents.lines().collect::<Vec<_>>();
2654 ... 377 
2655 ... 378     let mut excerpt = Vec::new();
2656 ... 379     let mut score = 0;
2657 ... 380     if !query_terms.is_empty() {
2658 ... 381         for (index, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {
2659 ... 382             let normalized = line.to_ascii_lowercase();
2660 ... 383             let matched_terms = query_terms
2661 ... 384                 .iter()
2662 ... 385                 .filter(|term| normalized.contains(term.as_str()))
2663 ... 386                 .count();
2664 ... 387             if matched_terms > 0 {
2665 ... 388                 score += matched_terms;
2666 ... 389                 let start = index.saturating_sub(1);
2667 ... 390                 let end = usize::min(index + 3, lines.len());
2668 ... 391                 excerpt.extend(lines[start..end].iter().copied());
2669 ... 392                 if excerpt.len() >= 8 {
2670 ... 393                     break;
2671 ... 394                 }
2672 ... 395             }
2673 ... 396         }
2674 ... 397     }
2675 ... 398 
2676 ... 399     if excerpt.is_empty() {
2677 ... 400         excerpt.extend(
2678 ... 401             lines
2679 ... 402                 .into_iter()
2680 ... 403                 .filter(|line| !line.trim().is_empty())
2681 ... 404                 .take(8),
2682 ... 405         );
2683 ... 406     }
2684 ... 407 
2685 ... 408     (trim_memory_contents(&excerpt.join("\n")), score)
2686 ... 409 }
2687 ... 410 
2688 ... 411 fn prompt_terms(user_prompt: &str) -> Vec<String> {
2689 ... 412     let mut terms = user_prompt
2690 ... 413         .to_ascii_lowercase()
2691 ... 414         .split(|ch: char| !ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric() && ch != '_' && ch != '.')
2692 ... 415         .filter(|term| term.len() >= 3)
2693 ... 416         .filter(|term| {
2694 ... 417             !matches!(
2695 ... 418                 *term,
2696 ... 419                 "the"
2697 ... 420                     | "and"
2698 ... 421                     | "with"
2699 ... 422                     | "from"
2700 ... 423                     | "into"
2701 ... 424                     | "that"
2702 ... 425                     | "this"
2703 ... 426                     | "what"
2704 ... 427                     | "when"
2705 ... 428                     | "where"
2706 ... 429                     | "which"
2707 ... 430                     | "would"
2708 ... 431                     | "could"
2709 ... 432                     | "should"
2710 ... 433                     | "about"
2711 ... 434                     | "your"
2712 ... 435             )
2713 ... 436         })
2714 ... 437         .map(str::to_string)
2715 ... 438         .collect::<Vec<_>>();
2716 ... 439     terms.sort();
2717 ... 440     terms.dedup();
2718 ... 441     terms
2719 ... 442 }

3181 .... 1996 fn format_planner_loop_state_digest(request: &PlannerRequest) -> String {
3182 .... 1997     let remaining_steps = request
3183 .... 1998         .budget
3184 .... 1999         .max_steps
3185 .... 2000         .saturating_sub(request.loop_state.steps.len());
3186 .... 2001     let mut lines = vec![format!(
3187 .... 2002         "Budget remaining: steps={}, evidence_limit={}, pending_branches={}",
3188 .... 2003         remaining_steps,
3189 .... 2004         request.budget.max_evidence_items,
3190 .... 2005         request.loop_state.pending_branches.len()
3191 .... 2006     )];
3192 .... 2007 
3193 .... 2008     if request.loop_state.steps.is_empty() {
3194 .... 2009         lines.push("No planner steps have executed yet.".to_string());
3195 .... 2010     } else {
3196 .... 2011         for step in request.loop_state.steps.iter().rev().take(4).rev() {
3197 .... 2012             lines.push(format!(
3198 .... 2013                 "- step {}: {} -> {}",
3199 .... 2014                 step.sequence,
3200 .... 2015                 step.action.summary(),
3201 .... 2016                 trim_for_context(&step.outcome, 180)
3202 .... 2017             ));
3203 .... 2018         }
3204 .... 2019     }
3205 .... 2020 
3206 .... 2021     if !request.loop_state.evidence_items.is_empty() {
3207 .... 2022         lines.push("Current evidence:".to_string());
3208 .... 2023         for item in request
3209 .... 2024             .loop_state
3210 .... 2025             .evidence_items
3211 .... 2026             .iter()
3212 .... 2027             .take(request.budget.max_evidence_items.min(4))
3213 .... 2028         {
3214 .... 2029             lines.push(format!(
3215 .... 2030                 "- {}: {}",
3216 .... 2031                 item.source,
3217 .... 2032                 trim_for_context(&item.snippet, 180)
3218 .... 2033             ));
3219 .... 2034         }
3220 .... 2035     }
3221 .... 2036 
3222 .... 2037     if !request.loop_state.notes.is_empty() {
3223 .... 2038         lines.push("Current notes:".to_string());
3224 .... 2039         for note in request.loop_state.notes.iter().take(3) {
3225 .... 2040             lines.push(format!("- {}", trim_for_context(note, 180)));
3226 .... 2041         }
3227 .... 2042     }
3228 .... 2043 
3229 .... 2044     if !request.loop_state.pending_branches.is_empty() {
3230 .... 2045         lines.push(format!(

...  570     async fn execute_recursive_planner_loop(
...  571         &self,
...  572         prompt: &str,
...  573         context: PlannerLoopContext,
...  574         event_sink: Arc<dyn TurnEventSink>,
...  575     ) -> Result<Option<EvidenceBundle>> {
...  576         let budget = PlannerBudget::default();
...  577         let mut loop_state = PlannerLoopState::default();
...  578         let mut used_workspace_resources = false;
...  579         let mut stop_reason = None;
...  580         let gatherer_provider = context
...  581             .prepared
...  582             .gatherer
...  583             .as_ref()
...  584             .map(|lane| lane.label.clone())
...  585             .unwrap_or_else(|| "workspace".to_string());
...  586 
...  587         for sequence in 1..=budget.max_steps {
...  588             let request = PlannerRequest::new(
...  589                 prompt,
...  590                 self.workspace_root.clone(),
...  591                 context.interpretation.clone(),
...  592                 budget.clone(),
...  593             )
...  594             .with_recent_turns(context.recent_turns.clone())
...  595             .with_loop_state(loop_state.clone());
...  596             let decision = context.planner_engine.select_next_action(&request).await?;
...  597             event_sink.emit(TurnEvent::PlannerActionSelected {
...  598                 sequence,
...  599                 action: decision.action.summary(),
...  600                 rationale: decision.rationale.clone(),
...  601             });
...  602 
...  603             let outcome = match &decision.action {
...  604                 PlannerAction::Search { query, intent } => {
...  605                     if let Some(gatherer) = context.gatherer.as_ref() {
...  606                         event_sink.emit(TurnEvent::GathererCapability {
...  607                             provider: gatherer_provider.clone(),
...  608                             capability: format_gatherer_capability(&gatherer.capability()),
...  609                         });

...  615                                     intent
...  616                                         .clone()

...  618                                     EvidenceBudget::default(),

...  620                                 .with_planning(PlannerConfig::default().with_step_limit(1))
...  621                                 .with_prior_context(
...  622                                     build_planner_prior_context(

...  627                                 );

...  649                                                 });

...  654                                                 budget.max_evidence_items,

...  657                                             used_workspace_resources = true;

...  661                                         }
...  662                                     }

...  664                                 }
...  665                             }
...  666                             GathererCapability::Unsupported { reason }

...  669                             }
...  670                         }
...  671                     } else {
...  672                         "no gatherer backend is configured for planner search".to_string()
...  673                     }
...  674                 }

...  694                 }

...  714                 }

...  716                     if let Some(gatherer) = context.gatherer.as_ref() {

... 262 
... 263 fn discover_linked_documents(agent_path: &Path, contents: &str) -> Vec<PathBuf> {
... 264     let mut ordered = Vec::new();
... 265     let mut seen = HashSet::new();
... 266     for target in extract_markdown_link_targets(contents)
... 267         .into_iter()
... 268         .chain(extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents))
... 269     {
... 270         let Some(resolved) = resolve_link_target(agent_path, &target) else {
... 271             continue;
... 272         };
... 273         let canonical = canonical_memory_path(&resolved);
... 274         if seen.insert(canonical) {
... 275             ordered.push(resolved);
... 276         }
... 277     }
... 278     ordered
... 279 }
... 280 
... 281 fn extract_markdown_link_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
... 282     let mut targets = Vec::new();
... 283     let mut remainder = contents;
... 284     while let Some(start) = remainder.find("](") {
... 285         let candidate = &remainder[start + 2..];
... 286         let Some(end) = candidate.find(')') else {
... 287             break;
... 288         };
... 289         let target = candidate[..end].trim();
... 290         if !target.is_empty() {
... 291             targets.push(target.to_string());
... 292         }
... 293         remainder = &candidate[end + 1..];
... 294     }
... 295     targets
... 296 }
... 297 
... 298 fn extract_backticked_doc_targets(contents: &str) -> Vec<String> {
... 299     let mut targets = Vec::new();
... 300     let mut in_tick = false;
... 301     let mut current = String::new();
... 302 
... 303     for ch in contents.chars() {
... 304         if ch == '`' {
... 305             if in_tick {
... 306                 let trimmed = current.trim();
... 307                 if looks_like_local_doc_target(trimmed) {
... 308                     targets.push(trimmed.to_string());
... 309                 }
... 310                 current.clear();
... 311             }
... 312             in_tick = !in_tick;
... 313             continue;
... 314         }
... 315 
... 316         if in_tick {
... 317             current.push(ch);
... 318         }
... 319     }
... 320 
... 321     targets
... 322 }
... 323 
... 324 fn looks_like_local_doc_target(target: &str) -> bool {
... 325     target.ends_with(".md") || target.starts_with(".keel/")
... 326 }
... 327 
... 328 fn resolve_link_target(agent_path: &Path, target: &str) -> Option<PathBuf> {
... 329     if target.starts_with("http://")
... 330         || target.starts_with("https://")
... 331         || target.starts_with("mailto:")
... 332     {
... 333         return None;
... 334     }
... 335 
... 336     let target = target.split('#').next()?.trim();
... 337     if target.is_empty() || !looks_like_local_doc_target(target) {
... 338         return None;
... 339     }
... 340 
... 341     let candidate = if Path::new(target).is_absolute() {
... 342         PathBuf::from(target)
... 343     } else {
... 344         agent_path.parent()?.join(target)
... 345     };
... 346 
... 347     if candidate.is_file() {
... 348         Some(candidate)
... 349     } else {
... 350         None
... 351     }
... 352 }

160 354 fn trim_memory_contents(contents: &str) -> String {
161 355     if contents.chars().count() <= MAX_MEMORY_FILE_CHARS {

src/infrastructure/adapters/agent_memory.rs --- 8/9 --- Rust
170 364     trimmed
171 365 }

... 367 fn display_path(workspace_root: &Path, path: &Path) -> String {
... 368     path.strip_prefix(workspace_root)
... 369         .unwrap_or(path)
... 370         .display()
... 371         .to_string()
... 372 }
... 373 
... 374 fn select_relevant_excerpt(contents: &str, user_prompt: &str) -> (String, usize) {
... 375     let query_terms = prompt_terms(user_prompt);
... 376     let lines = contents.lines().collect::<Vec<_>>();
... 377 
... 378     let mut excerpt = Vec::new();
... 379     let mut score = 0;
... 380     if !query_terms.is_empty() {
... 381         for (index, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {
... 382             let normalized = line.to_ascii_lowercase();
... 383             let matched_terms = query_terms
... 384                 .iter()
... 385                 .filter(|term| normalized.contains(term.as_str()))
... 386                 .count();
... 387             if matched_terms > 0 {
... 388                 score += matched_terms;
... 389                 let start = index.saturating_sub(1);
... 390                 let end = usize::min(index + 3, lines.len());
... 391                 excerpt.extend(lines[start..end].iter().copied());
... 392                 if excerpt.len() >= 8 {
... 393                     break;
... 394                 }
... 395             }
... 396         }
... 397     }
... 398 
... 399     if excerpt.is_empty() {
... 400         excerpt.extend(
... 401             lines
... 402                 .into_iter()
... 403                 .filter(|line| !line.trim().is_empty())
... 404                 .take(8),
... 405         );
... 406     }
... 407 
... 408     (trim_memory_contents(&excerpt.join("\n")), score)
... 409 }
... 410 
... 411 fn prompt_terms(user_prompt: &str) -> Vec<String> {
... 412     let mut terms = user_prompt
... 413         .to_ascii_lowercase()
... 414         .split(|ch: char| !ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric() && ch != '_' && ch != '.')
... 415         .filter(|term| term.len() >= 3)
... 416         .filter(|term| {
... 417             !matches!(
... 418                 *term,
... 419                 "the"
... 420                     | "and"
... 421                     | "with"
... 422                     | "from"
... 423                     | "into"
... 424                     | "that"
... 425                     | "this"
... 426                     | "what"
... 427                     | "when"
... 428                     | "where"
... 429                     | "which"
... 430                     | "would"
... 431                     | "could"
... 432                     | "should"
... 433                     | "about"
... 434                     | "your"
... 435             )
... 436         })
... 437         .map(str::to_string)
... 438         .collect::<Vec<_>>();
... 439     terms.sort();
... 440     terms.dedup();
... 441     terms
... 442 }

.... 1996 fn format_planner_loop_state_digest(request: &PlannerRequest) -> String {
.... 1997     let remaining_steps = request
.... 1998         .budget
.... 1999         .max_steps
.... 2000         .saturating_sub(request.loop_state.steps.len());
.... 2001     let mut lines = vec![format!(
.... 2002         "Budget remaining: steps={}, evidence_limit={}, pending_branches={}",
.... 2003         remaining_steps,
.... 2004         request.budget.max_evidence_items,
.... 2005         request.loop_state.pending_branches.len()
.... 2006     )];
.... 2007 
.... 2008     if request.loop_state.steps.is_empty() {
.... 2009         lines.push("No planner steps have executed yet.".to_string());
.... 2010     } else {
.... 2011         for step in request.loop_state.steps.iter().rev().take(4).rev() {
.... 2012             lines.push(format!(
.... 2013                 "- step {}: {} -> {}",
.... 2014                 step.sequence,
.... 2015                 step.action.summary(),
.... 2016                 trim_for_context(&step.outcome, 180)
.... 2017             ));
.... 2018         }
.... 2019     }
.... 2020 
.... 2021     if !request.loop_state.evidence_items.is_empty() {
.... 2022         lines.push("Current evidence:".to_string());
.... 2023         for item in request
.... 2024             .loop_state
.... 2025             .evidence_items
.... 2026             .iter()
.... 2027             .take(request.budget.max_evidence_items.min(4))
.... 2028         {
.... 2029             lines.push(format!(
.... 2030                 "- {}: {}",
.... 2031                 item.source,
.... 2032                 trim_for_context(&item.snippet, 180)
.... 2033             ));
.... 2034         }
.... 2035     }
.... 2036 
.... 2037     if !request.loop_state.notes.is_empty() {
.... 2038         lines.push("Current notes:".to_string());
.... 2039         for note in request.loop_state.notes.iter().take(3) {
.... 2040             lines.push(format!("- {}", trim_for_context(note, 180)));
.... 2041         }
.... 2042     }
.... 2043 
.... 2044     if !request.loop_state.pending_branches.is_empty() {
.... 2045         lines.push(format!(
.... 2046             "Pending branches: {}",
.... 2047             request.loop_state.pending_branches.join(" | ")
.... 2048         ));
.... 2049     }
.... 2050 
.... 2051     lines.join("\n")
.... 2052 }

.... 2296 ) -> Result<RecursivePlannerDecision> {

.... 2302         } => RecursivePlannerDecision {

.... 2308                 }),

.... 2311         },
.... 2312         PlannerActionEnvelope::Read { path, rationale } => RecursivePlannerDecision {

.... 2315             },
.... 2316             rationale: required_planner_field("rationale", rationale)?,
.... 2317         },
.... 2318         PlannerActionEnvelope::Inspect { command, rationale } => RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2319             action: PlannerAction::Inspect {
.... 2320                 command: required_planner_field("command", command)?,
.... 2321             },
.... 2322             rationale: required_planner_field("rationale", rationale)?,
.... 2323         },
.... 2324         PlannerActionEnvelope::Refine { query, rationale } => {
.... 2325             let rationale_text = rationale
.... 2326                 .as_deref()
.... 2327                 .map(str::trim)
.... 2328                 .filter(|value| !value.is_empty())
.... 2329                 .map(str::to_string);
.... 2330             RecursivePlannerDecision {
.... 2331                 action: PlannerAction::Refine {
.... 2332                     query: required_planner_field("query", query)?,
.... 2333                     rationale: rationale_text.clone(),
.... 2334                 },
.... 2335                 rationale: rationale_text.unwrap_or_else(|| "refine the investigation".to_string()),
.... 2336             }
.... 2337         }
.... 2338         PlannerActionEnvelope::Branch {
.... 2339             branches,
.... 2340             rationale,
.... 2341         } => {
.... 2342             let branches = branches
